<title>Sales Representative (Us Office) Glocalize   Los Angeles, Ca   </title>
<pubDate>Sat, 29 Apr 2023 09:36:42 +0000</pubDate>
<dc:creator>Freelance</dc:creator>
<guid isPermaLink="true">None</guid>
<description><![CDATA[<div class="separator"><div style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img alt='Field Sales (Outside Sales) Representative job description template |  Workable' src='https://encrypted-tbn0.gstatic.com/images?q=tbn:ANd9GcRQEXcfQ7yJ46Q7y6PmhNbMRAGcumBPBXUQBw&usqp=CAU' width='640' height='229' /></div></div><br /><br /><br /><b>Sales Representative (US Office) Glocalize   Los Angeles, CA   </b>  <h3>Overview:</h3> <blockquote><i>Full-time
No degree mentioned<br/> Glocalize<br/>  Los Angeles, CA   </i></blockquote><h3>Responsibilities:</h3> <div class"jobresponsibilities"> A successful candidate that we are looking for is a highly motivated individual who can work professionally and autonomously in a fast-paced environment
This individual candidate, which will be based in our Singapore office, must have strong communication skills with the right mix of organizational and prioritization skills; a great team player and a self-starter
Proven sales records and relevant experience in the localization media industry
Familiarity with relationship management practices along with the ability to build productive business professional relationships
Highly motivated and target-driven with a proven track record in sales
Excellent selling, negotiation, and communication skills
Prioritizing, time management, and organizational skills
Ability to work independently and with the team
Ability to create and deliver sales deck tailored to the clients' needs
Relationship management skills and openness to feedback
Excellent verbal and written English communication skills
Problem-solving capabilities
Quality and detail-oriented
Self-starter and proactive
Ability to meet deadlines under pressure
Knowledge of an additional language is an advantage
We are looking for a results-driven Sales Representative, who will be responsible for communicating the benefits of our products and services in order to drive sales
This role is required to provide a comprehensive and appropriate localization solution for every customer to boost top-line revenue growth, expand the customer base, and overall profitability of the organization
Present, promote, and sell our products and/or services using solid arguments to existing and prospective clients
Perform cost-benefit and analysis of existing/potential customers to meet their requirements
Establish, develop and maintain positive business and client relationships
Reach out to clients and generate leads through cold calling and emailing
Work together with the team to expedite the resolution of customer problems and complaints
Achieve and meet sales targets and outcomes within the given schedule
Coordinate sales effort with other team members and other departments
Analyze the territory/market’s potential, track sales and status reports
Supply sales reports on customer needs, problems, interests, competitive activities, and potential for new products and services
Keep abreast of best practices and trends in the localization industries
Continuously improve through client's and peer's feedback</div><br /><div class="separator"><div style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img alt='Contact Us | Sales Rep| Butler Human Services Furniture' src='https://encrypted-tbn0.gstatic.com/images?q=tbn:ANd9GcSidV-4TUFml7AdfIEb3NTjr73nMCj7k8reMg&usqp=CAU' width='640' height='398' /></div></div><br /><br /><br /> <h3>Job Description:</h3> <div class"jobdescription">Sales Representative (US Office)

GloZ is inviting professionals to join the League ...


GloZ is a globalization company that helps entertainment companies, content creators, producers, and artists around the world to expand their boundaries beyond languages and cultures. Our vision is to bring the world together by empowering stories, as we believe that everyone and every business has its own stories. Our mission is to spread fun, love, laughter, tears, and knowledge by glocalizing great stories around the world.

At GloZ, we have an opening for an ace team member to join our amazing League. A successful candidate that we are looking for is a highly motivated individual who can work professionally and autonomously in a fast-paced environment. This individual candidate, which will be based in our Singapore office, must have strong communication skills with the right mix of organizational and prioritization skills; a great team player and a self-starter.

Sales Representative Job Summary

We are looking for a results-driven Sales Representative, who will be responsible for communicating the benefits of our products and services in order to drive sales. Excellent interpersonal skills and the ability to engage clients' prospects and relationships are crucial for this position. Experience working with a global fun team and a track record of excellent customer service are huge pluses as well.

This role is required to provide a comprehensive and appropriate localization solution for every customer to boost top-line revenue growth, expand the customer base, and overall profitability of the organization.
<H4>
Key Responsibilities</H4>
<ul>
<li>Present, promote, and sell our products and/or services using solid arguments to existing and prospective clients.</li>
<li>Perform cost-benefit and analysis of existing/potential customers to meet their requirements.</li>
<li>Establish, develop and maintain positive business and client relationships.</li>
<li>Reach out to clients and generate leads through cold calling and emailing.</li>
<li>Work together with the team to expedite the resolution of customer problems and complaints.</li>
<li>Achieve and meet sales targets and outcomes within the given schedule.</li>
<li>Coordinate sales effort with other team members and other departments.</li>
<li>Analyze the territory/market’s potential, track sales and status reports.</li>
<li>Supply sales reports on customer needs, problems, interests, competitive activities, and potential for new products and services.</li>
<li>Keep abreast of best practices and trends in the localization industries.</li>
<li>Continuously improve through client's and peer's feedback.</li>
</ul><H4>
Requirements</H4>
<ul>
<li>Proven sales records and relevant experience in the localization media industry</li>
<li>Familiarity with relationship management practices along with the ability to build productive business professional relationships</li>
<li>Highly motivated and target-driven with a proven track record in sales</li>
<li>Excellent selling, negotiation, and communication skills</li>
<li>Prioritizing, time management, and organizational skills</li>
<li>Ability to work independently and with the team</li>
<li>Ability to create and deliver sales deck tailored to the clients' needs</li>
<li>Relationship management skills and openness to feedback</li>
</ul><H4>
Skills and Abilities</H4>
<ul>
<li>Excellent verbal and written English communication skills</li>
<li>Organizational skills</li>
<li>Problem-solving capabilities</li>
<li>Quality and detail-oriented</li>
<li>Self-starter and proactive</li>
<li>Ability to meet deadlines under pressure</li>
</ul>• Knowledge of an additional language is an advantage</div> <br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/>Summary:<br/><div class="jobsummary">Coordinate sales effort with other team members and other departments.. Supply sales reports on customer needs, problems, interests, competitive activities, and potential for new products and services
Keep abreast of best practices and trends in the localization industries
Continuously improve through client's and peer's feedback</div><br /><div class="separator"><div style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img alt='Contact Us | Sales Rep| Butler Human Services Furniture' src='https://encrypted-tbn0.gstatic.com/images?q=tbn:ANd9GcSidV-4TUFml7AdfIEb3NTjr73nMCj7k8reMg&usqp=CAU' width='640' height='398' /></div></div><br /><br /><br /> <h3>Job Description:</h3> <div class"jobdescription">Sales Representative (US Office)

GloZ is inviting professionals to join the League ...


GloZ is a globalization company that helps entertainment companies, content creators, producers, and artists around the world to expand their boundaries beyond languages and cultures. Our vision is to bring the world together by empowering stories, as we believe that everyone and every business has its own stories. Our mission is to spread fun, love, laughter, tears, and knowledge by glocalizing great stories around the world.

At GloZ, we have an opening for an ace team member to join our amazing League. A successful candidate that we are looking for is a highly motivated individual who can work professionally and autonomously in a fast-paced environment. This individual candidate, which will be based in our Singapore office, must have strong communication skills with the right mix of organizational and prioritization skills; a great team player and a self-starter.

Sales Representative Job Summary

We are looking for a results-driven Sales Representative, who will be responsible for communicating the benefits of our products and services in order to drive sales. Excellent interpersonal skills and the ability to engage clients' prospects and relationships are crucial for this position. Experience working with a global fun team and a track record of excellent customer service are huge pluses as well.

This role is required to provide a comprehensive and appropriate localization solution for every customer to boost top-line revenue growth, expand the customer base, and overall profitability of the organization.
<H4>
Key Responsibilities</H4>
<ul>
<li>Present, promote, and sell our products and/or services using solid arguments to existing and prospective clients.</li>
<li>Perform cost-benefit and analysis of existing/potential customers to meet their requirements.</li>
<li>Establish, develop and maintain positive business and client relationships.</li>
<li>Reach out to clients and generate leads through cold calling and emailing.</li>
<li>Work together with the team to expedite the resolution of customer problems and complaints.</li>
<li>Achieve and meet sales targets and outcomes within the given schedule.</li>
<li>Coordinate sales effort with other team members and other departments.</li>
<li>Analyze the territory/market’s potential, track sales and status reports.</li>
<li>Supply sales reports on customer needs, problems, interests, competitive activities, and potential for new products and services.</li>
<li>Keep abreast of best practices and trends in the localization industries.</li>
<li>Continuously improve through client's and peer's feedback.</li>
</ul><H4>
Requirements</H4>
<ul>
<li>Proven sales records and relevant experience in the localization media industry</li>
<li>Familiarity with relationship management practices along with the ability to build productive business professional relationships</li>
<li>Highly motivated and target-driven with a proven track record in sales</li>
<li>Excellent selling, negotiation, and communication skills</li>
<li>Prioritizing, time management, and organizational skills</li>
<li>Ability to work independently and with the team</li>
<li>Ability to create and deliver sales deck tailored to the clients' needs</li>
<li>Relationship management skills and openness to feedback</li>
</ul><H4>
Skills and Abilities</H4>
<ul>
<li>Excellent verbal and written English communication skills</li>
<li>Organizational skills</li>
<li>Problem-solving capabilities</li>
<li>Quality and detail-oriented</li>
<li>Self-starter and proactive</li>
<li>Ability to meet deadlines under pressure</li>
</ul>• Knowledge of an additional language is an advantage</div> <br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/>Summary:<br/><div class="jobsummary">Coordinate sales effort with other team members and other departments.. <description><![CDATA[<b>Range Cowboy 1 (ZX Ranch) Simplot   Paisley, OR   </b>  <h3>Overview:</h3> <blockquote><i>No degree mentioned
Full-time<br/> Simplot<br/>  Paisley, OR   </i></blockquote><h3>Responsibilities:</h3> <div class"jobresponsibilities"> Reasonable accommodations may be made to enable individuals with disabilities to perform the essential functions

The employee occasionally works near moving mechanical parts and is occasionally exposed to wet and/or humid conditions</div> <h3>Job Description:</h3> <div class"jobdescription">The J.R. Simplot Company is a diverse, privately held organization, with roots firmly planted in agriculture and agriculture-related businesses. The J.R. Simplot Company is a true farm-to-table company with operations that touch every aspect of agriculture, including seed production, farming and ranching, plant sciences, fertilizer manufacturing, food processing, commercial product development ...
 and distribution.

SUMMARY
Assists Ranch Manager and Staff Veterinarian in the care and treatment of range cattle and/or cow-calf operations by performing the following duties.

ESSENTIAL DUTIES AND RESPONSIBILITIES include the following. Other duties may be assigned.

Rides on horseback in order to identify sick, injured, or stressed animals; gathers cattle on range and pasture; calves cows; supplements feed during winter; repairs pasture and range fences.

Assists in treating sick or injured cattle by following an established medical treatment plan provided by the Staff Veterinarian and/or Ranch Manager/Foreman.

Assists with processing and shipping cattle by sorting, branding, vaccinating, worming, and tagging.

Moves cattle from pasture to pasture as directed by the Ranch Manager/Foreman.

Provides care to horses by shoeing, doctoring, feeding, and grooming as necessary.

Performs other duties as assigned by the Ranch Manager/Foreman.

QUALIFICATIONS To perform this job successfully, an individual must be able to perform each essential duty satisfactorily. The requirements listed below are representative of the knowledge, skill, and/or ability required. Reasonable accommodations may be made to enable individuals with disabilities to perform the essential functions.

EDUCATION and/or EXPERIENCE
Knowledgeable in the areas of animal health and cattle conditions generally acquired with a minimum of four to five years related experience and/or training.

LANGUAGE SKILLS
Ability to read and comprehend simple instructions, short correspondence, and memos. Ability to write simple correspondence. Ability to effectively present information in one-on-one and small group situations to customers, clients, and other employees of the organization.

MATHEMATICAL SKILLS
Ability to add and subtract two digit numbers and to multiply and divide with 10's and 100's. Ability to perform these operations using units of American money and weight measurement, volume, and distance.

REASONING ABILITY
Ability to apply commonsense understanding to carry out detailed but uninvolved written or oral instructions. Ability to deal with problems involving a few concrete variables in standardized situations.

CERTIFICATES, LICENSES, REGISTRATIONS
Must be a licensed driver of single axle vehicles.

OTHER SKILLS AND ABILITIES
Ability to saddle and ride a horse. Must provide own tack.

PHYSICAL DEMANDS The physical demands described here are representative of those that must be met by an employee to successfully perform the essential functions of this job. Reasonable accommodations may be made to enable individuals with disabilities to perform the essential functions.

While performing the duties of this job, the employee is regularly required to sit and reach with hands and arms. The employee frequently is required to stand; walk; and use hands/fingers to handle, manipulate, or feel objects, tools, or controls. The employee is occasionally required to stoop, kneel, crouch, or crawl. The employee must frequently lift and/or move up to 50 pounds and occasionally lift and/or move more than 100 pounds. Specific vision abilities required by this job include distance vision, color vision, and depth perception.

WORK ENVIRONMENT The work environment characteristics described here are representative of those an employee encounters while performing the essential functions of this job. Reasonable accommodations may be made to enable individuals with disabilities to perform the essential functions.

While performing the duties of this job, the employee regularly works in outside weather conditions and is regularly exposed to fumes or airborne particles. The employee occasionally works near moving mechanical parts and is occasionally exposed to wet and/or humid conditions. The noise level in the work environment is usually moderate.

Job Requisition ID: 13535

Travel Required: None

Location(s): L&L ZX Ranch - Paisley

Country: United States

The J.R. Simplot Company is proud to be an Equal Opportunity Employer and will consider all qualified applicants for employment without regard to race, color, religion, national origin, ancestry, age, sex, gender, gender identity, gender expression, genetic information, physical or mental disability, medical condition, sexual orientation, military or veteran status, marital status, or any other protected status</div> <br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/>Summary:<br/><div class="jobsummary">Specific vision abilities required by this job include distance vision color vision and depth perception.. The employee occasionally works near moving mechanical parts and is occasionally exposed to wet and/or humid conditions</div> <h3>Job Description:</h3> <div class"jobdescription">The J.R. Simplot Company is a diverse, privately held organization, with roots firmly planted in agriculture and agriculture-related businesses. The J.R. Simplot Company is a true farm-to-table company with operations that touch every aspect of agriculture, including seed production, farming and ranching, plant sciences, fertilizer manufacturing, food processing, commercial product development ...
 and distribution.

SUMMARY
Assists Ranch Manager and Staff Veterinarian in the care and treatment of range cattle and/or cow-calf operations by performing the following duties.

ESSENTIAL DUTIES AND RESPONSIBILITIES include the following. Other duties may be assigned.

Rides on horseback in order to identify sick, injured, or stressed animals; gathers cattle on range and pasture; calves cows; supplements feed during winter; repairs pasture and range fences.

Assists in treating sick or injured cattle by following an established medical treatment plan provided by the Staff Veterinarian and/or Ranch Manager/Foreman.

Assists with processing and shipping cattle by sorting, branding, vaccinating, worming, and tagging.

Moves cattle from pasture to pasture as directed by the Ranch Manager/Foreman.

Provides care to horses by shoeing, doctoring, feeding, and grooming as necessary.

Performs other duties as assigned by the Ranch Manager/Foreman.

QUALIFICATIONS To perform this job successfully, an individual must be able to perform each essential duty satisfactorily. The requirements listed below are representative of the knowledge, skill, and/or ability required. Reasonable accommodations may be made to enable individuals with disabilities to perform the essential functions.

EDUCATION and/or EXPERIENCE
Knowledgeable in the areas of animal health and cattle conditions generally acquired with a minimum of four to five years related experience and/or training.

LANGUAGE SKILLS
Ability to read and comprehend simple instructions, short correspondence, and memos. Ability to write simple correspondence. Ability to effectively present information in one-on-one and small group situations to customers, clients, and other employees of the organization.

MATHEMATICAL SKILLS
Ability to add and subtract two digit numbers and to multiply and divide with 10's and 100's. Ability to perform these operations using units of American money and weight measurement, volume, and distance.

REASONING ABILITY
Ability to apply commonsense understanding to carry out detailed but uninvolved written or oral instructions. Ability to deal with problems involving a few concrete variables in standardized situations.

CERTIFICATES, LICENSES, REGISTRATIONS
Must be a licensed driver of single axle vehicles.

OTHER SKILLS AND ABILITIES
Ability to saddle and ride a horse. Must provide own tack.

PHYSICAL DEMANDS The physical demands described here are representative of those that must be met by an employee to successfully perform the essential functions of this job. Reasonable accommodations may be made to enable individuals with disabilities to perform the essential functions.

While performing the duties of this job, the employee is regularly required to sit and reach with hands and arms. The employee frequently is required to stand; walk; and use hands/fingers to handle, manipulate, or feel objects, tools, or controls. The employee is occasionally required to stoop, kneel, crouch, or crawl. The employee must frequently lift and/or move up to 50 pounds and occasionally lift and/or move more than 100 pounds. Specific vision abilities required by this job include distance vision, color vision, and depth perception.

WORK ENVIRONMENT The work environment characteristics described here are representative of those an employee encounters while performing the essential functions of this job. Reasonable accommodations may be made to enable individuals with disabilities to perform the essential functions.

While performing the duties of this job, the employee regularly works in outside weather conditions and is regularly exposed to fumes or airborne particles. The employee occasionally works near moving mechanical parts and is occasionally exposed to wet and/or humid conditions. The noise level in the work environment is usually moderate.

Job Requisition ID: 13535

Travel Required: None

Location(s): L&L ZX Ranch - Paisley

Country: United States

Responsible for operating a 26' Box Truck while maintaining compliance with applicable federal, state and local laws and regulations as well as company policies
Fully understand how to operate and safely drive commercial vehicles with a GCWR of 26,001lbs or more, with a towed weight of less than 10,000lbs
Responsible for proper loading and securing of freight to prevent movement and allow safe transport
Assist in loading and loading as required
Willing to load/unload and assist in operations at the terminal as required

Perform and document pre-trip inspections, on-the-road inspection, and post-trip inspections
Maneuver and control the vehicle in a safe fashion, which includes handling the vehicle on-site and in over-the-road situations, proper signaling, searching for hazards, controlling speed, lane positioning, matching speeds to road conditions, and the ability to drive during the daytime or nighttime

Responsible for operating a 26' Box Truck while maintaining compliance with applicable federal, state and local laws and regulations as well as company policies ...


Key Responsibilities:

· Fully understand how to operate and safely drive commercial vehicles with a GCWR of 26,001lbs or more, with a towed weight of less than 10,000lbs.

· Responsible for proper loading and securing of freight to prevent movement and allow safe transport. Assist in loading and loading as required.

· Willing to load/unload and assist in operations at the terminal as required.

· Maintain accurate records and logs in accordance with DOT and company policy.

· Perform and document pre-trip inspections, on-the-road inspection, and post-trip inspections.

· Maneuver and control the vehicle in a safe fashion, which includes handling the vehicle on-site and in over-the-road situations, proper signaling, searching for hazards, controlling speed, lane positioning, matching speeds to road conditions, and the ability to drive during the daytime or nighttime.

· Knowledge and adherence to Hours-of-Service regulations, maintaining ELD/paper logs to track and report duty hours.

· Wiling to work stand by hours

· Keeping the vehicles interior and exterior clean and in good condition.

· Perform job functions in a safe manner to avoid personal injury and equipment damage

· Maintaining valid license and certifications.

· Any additional duties assigned

Job Type: Full-time

Pay: $19.00 - $22.00 per hour

Benefits:
<li>Dental insurance</li>
<li>Health insurance</li>
<li>Life insurance</li>
<li>Paid time off</li>
<li>Paid training</li>
<li>Referral program</li>

<li>Weekend availability</li>

<li>8 hour shift</li>

Responsible for operating a 26' Box Truck while maintaining compliance with applicable federal, state and local laws and regulations as well as company policies ...


Key Responsibilities:

· Fully understand how to operate and safely drive commercial vehicles with a GCWR of 26,001lbs or more, with a towed weight of less than 10,000lbs.

· Responsible for proper loading and securing of freight to prevent movement and allow safe transport. Assist in loading and loading as required.

· Willing to load/unload and assist in operations at the terminal as required.

· Maintain accurate records and logs in accordance with DOT and company policy.

· Perform and document pre-trip inspections, on-the-road inspection, and post-trip inspections.

· Maneuver and control the vehicle in a safe fashion, which includes handling the vehicle on-site and in over-the-road situations, proper signaling, searching for hazards, controlling speed, lane positioning, matching speeds to road conditions, and the ability to drive during the daytime or nighttime.

· Knowledge and adherence to Hours-of-Service regulations, maintaining ELD/paper logs to track and report duty hours.

· Wiling to work stand by hours

· Keeping the vehicles interior and exterior clean and in good condition.

· Perform job functions in a safe manner to avoid personal injury and equipment damage

· Maintaining valid license and certifications.

· Any additional duties assigned

Job Type: Full-time

Pay: $19.00 - $22.00 per hour

The World Headquarters for the Dallas Cowboys, the Star is the most comprehensive NFL training facility in the country. In addition to serving as the home of the entire football operation and practice fields, The Ford Center at The Star also includes a multipurpose, 12,000 seat, indoor stadium that will provide facilities for use by the Dallas Cowboys, City of Frisco and Frisco ISD ...
 football and soccer games.

The facility includes Cowboys Club: a workspace and membership club connecting work, leisure and culture for a select community of influencers, entrepreneurs, and business leaders with a passion for the Dallas Cowboys.

The Barista is based out of The Star/Cowboys Club in Frisco, TX and reports to the Beverage Manager.
<H4>
Essential Job Functions
</H4>
<ul>
<li>Follows all Company drink recipes and procedures to provide high quality and consistent beverages to guest</li>

<li>Ensures that all customers are educated on our products and services.</li>

<li>Answers customer questions regarding coffee blends, preparation, and product freshness.</li>

<li>Greets all customers with fast, friendly, personalized service</li>

<li>Accurately rings sales orders into POS system and counts back change to customers in a courteous and friendly manner</li>

<li>Develops an understanding of coffee and tea regions and the various differences in flavor and blends.</li>

<li>Sells and serves baked goods and miscellaneous food items to customers</li>

<li>Maintains a clean and organized workspace so that partners can locate resources and product as needed</li>

<li>Other duties as assigned</li>
</ul>
Knowledge, Skills and Ability

The individual must possess the following knowledge, skills and abilities and be able to explain and demonstrate that he or she can perform the essential functions of the job, with or without reasonable accommodation.

<li>Excellent customer service</li>

<li>Can be trusted to act in a manner that is truthful and values direct, honest communication at all levels of the organization</li>

<li>Strong interpersonal skills; can effectively communicate and relate to all levels within and outside the organization; creates and builds positive and productive relationships</li>

<li>Responds quickly and effectively to changing trends and circumstances; embraces change and welcomes fresh perspectives; learns from past mistakes and adjusts accordingly</li>

<li>Ability to manage appropriate steps to get projects completed; has strong abilities to organize people and processes; can create a plan for resourceful workflow</li>

<li>Can manage people and resources to get projects completed; has a strong ability to multi-task and keep order.</li>

<li>Detail Oriented</li>

<li>Ability to work independently and/or in a team environment</li>

<li>Strong verbal and written communication skills</li>

<li>Must have computer skills:</li>
Microsoft Word, Excel.

<li>Must be able to stand for an extended period of time without aid</li>

<li>Menu planning and development</li>

<li>Must be able to stand or walk for varying length of time</li>

<li>Must be available to work an irregular schedule</li>

<li>Must be able to work extended hours due to business requirements including late nights, weekends and holidays.</li>

Preferred

Qualifications:

<li>Must have at least 1 year experience in a high volume bar.</li>

Physical Requirements:

The World Headquarters for the Dallas Cowboys, the Star is the most comprehensive NFL training facility in the country. In addition to serving as the home of the entire football operation and practice fields, The Ford Center at The Star also includes a multipurpose, 12,000 seat, indoor stadium that will provide facilities for use by the Dallas Cowboys, City of Frisco and Frisco ISD ...
 football and soccer games.

The facility includes Cowboys Club: a workspace and membership club connecting work, leisure and culture for a select community of influencers, entrepreneurs, and business leaders with a passion for the Dallas Cowboys.

The Barista is based out of The Star/Cowboys Club in Frisco, TX and reports to the Beverage Manager.
<H4>
Essential Job Functions
</H4>
<ul>
<li>Follows all Company drink recipes and procedures to provide high quality and consistent beverages to guest</li>

<li>Ensures that all customers are educated on our products and services.</li>

<li>Answers customer questions regarding coffee blends, preparation, and product freshness.</li>

<li>Greets all customers with fast, friendly, personalized service</li>

<li>Accurately rings sales orders into POS system and counts back change to customers in a courteous and friendly manner</li>

<li>Develops an understanding of coffee and tea regions and the various differences in flavor and blends.</li>

<li>Sells and serves baked goods and miscellaneous food items to customers</li>

<li>Maintains a clean and organized workspace so that partners can locate resources and product as needed</li>

<li>Other duties as assigned</li>
</ul>
Knowledge, Skills and Ability

The individual must possess the following knowledge, skills and abilities and be able to explain and demonstrate that he or she can perform the essential functions of the job, with or without reasonable accommodation.

<li>Excellent customer service</li>

<li>Can be trusted to act in a manner that is truthful and values direct, honest communication at all levels of the organization</li>

<li>Strong interpersonal skills; can effectively communicate and relate to all levels within and outside the organization; creates and builds positive and productive relationships</li>

<li>Responds quickly and effectively to changing trends and circumstances; embraces change and welcomes fresh perspectives; learns from past mistakes and adjusts accordingly</li>

<li>Ability to manage appropriate steps to get projects completed; has strong abilities to organize people and processes; can create a plan for resourceful workflow</li>

<li>Can manage people and resources to get projects completed; has a strong ability to multi-task and keep order.</li>

<li>Detail Oriented</li>

<li>Ability to work independently and/or in a team environment</li>

<li>Strong verbal and written communication skills</li>

<li>Must have computer skills:</li>
Microsoft Word, Excel.

Required Qualifications:

<li>Must be able to stand for an extended period of time without aid</li>

<li>Must be fluent in English</li>

<li>Menu planning and development</li>

<li>Must be able to stand or walk for varying length of time</li>

<li>Must be available to work an irregular schedule</li>

<li>Must be able to work extended hours due to business requirements including late nights, weekends and holidays.</li>

Preferred

Qualifications:

<li>Must have at least 1 year experience in a high volume bar.</li>

<li>Must be able read, write, and speak in English.</li>

Physical Requirements:

<li>Ability to stand, sit, use of hands to handle, or feel, reach with hands and arms</li>

<li>Ability to lift and/ or move up to 25 pounds;</li>

<li>Specific vision abilities required by this job include close vision and distance vision</li>

Environmental

Working Conditions:

<li>The noise level in the work environment is usually moderate.</li>

Legends is an Equal Opportunity employer. All qualified applicants will receive consideration for employment without regard to race, color, religion, sex, age, national origin, disability, or genetic information.

<li>Must be able to stand or walk for varying length of time</li>

<li>Must be available to work an irregular schedule</li>

<li>Must be able to work extended hours due to business requirements including late nights, weekends and holidays.</li>

Preferred

Qualifications:

<li>Must have at least 1 year experience in a high volume bar.</li>

<li>Must be able read, write, and speak in English.</li>

Physical Requirements:

<li>Ability to stand, sit, use of hands to handle, or feel, reach with hands and arms</li>

<li>Ability to lift and/ or move up to 25 pounds;</li>

<li>Specific vision abilities required by this job include close vision and distance vision</li>

Environmental

Working Conditions:

<li>The noise level in the work environment is usually moderate.</li>

Legends is an Equal Opportunity employer. All qualified applicants will receive consideration for employment without regard to race, color, religion, sex, age, national origin, disability, or genetic information.

DLL

<title>Lowongan Kerja 2022 Karyawan Pabrik Via Online 2022 Pt Astra Group   Temanggung, Kabupaten Temanggung, Jawa Tengah   </title>
<pubDate>Wed, 03 May 2023 08:36:45 +0000</pubDate>
<dc:creator>Freelance</dc:creator>
<guid isPermaLink="true">None</guid>
<description><![CDATA[<div class="separator"><div style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img alt='Lowongan Kerja PT IMIP Agustus 2022, Cek Kualifikasi dan Syaratnya -  Tribunpalu.com' src='https://encrypted-tbn0.gstatic.com/images?q=tbn:ANd9GcRQIy0LtHN9p6mGid3U8Uoy7gc2BArW9k2gNQ&usqp=CAU' width='640' height='359' /></div></div><br /><br /><br /><b>LOWONGAN KERJA 2022 KARYAWAN PABRIK VIA ONLINE 2022 PT ASTRA GROUP   Temanggung, Kabupaten Temanggung, Jawa Tengah   </b>  <h3>Overview:</h3> <blockquote><i>Pekerjaan tetap<br/> PT ASTRA GROUP<br/>  Temanggung, Kabupaten Temanggung, Jawa Tengah   </i></blockquote><h3>Responsibilities:</h3> <div class"jobresponsibilities"> </div><br /><div class="separator"><div style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img alt='Lowongan Kerja: Indonesia — 32.000+ Lowongan Kerja Terbaru — Jooble' src='https://encrypted-tbn0.gstatic.com/images?q=tbn:ANd9GcQO01T6lsBA7vRrTUBD7F5NAT90_VhRhfdWZA&usqp=CAU' width='640' height='256' /></div></div><br /><br /><br /> <h3>Job Description:</h3> <div class"jobdescription">LOWONGAN KERJA 2022

||LOWONGAN KERJA PABRIK TERBARU|| LOKER SMA/SMK SEDERAJAT ||INFO LOWONGAN KERJA ASTRA GROUP TBK

LOWONGAN KERJA 2022 – PT Astra Group merupakan salah Satu Perusahaan Di bidang otomotif roda dua Dan empat terkemuka di Indonesia, Perusahaan ini Berdiri Pada Tahun 1957 setelah itu Sudah Menjadi Perusahaan Populer.

Hingga Pada tahun 1990, perusahaan mengubah nama menjadi PT Astra International Tbk.

PT Astra Group saat ini bergerak di bidang otomotif yang memproduksi Spare Part otomotif dan Perakitan Kendaraan Astra.Saat ini beberapa perusahaan yang bernaung di Astra Group di antaranya adalah :
<li>PT. ADM (Astra Daihatsu Motor)</li>
<li>PT. Toyota Astra Motor</li>
<li>PT. Astra Honda Motor (AHM)</li>
<li>PT. GS Baterai</li>
<li>PT. Showa Indonesia,</li>
<li>PT. Aisan Nasmoco Industri Manufaktur Otomotif,</li>
<li>dan masih banyak yang lainnya</li>

Guna mengisi beberapa posisi/bagian yang kosong maka perusahaan Astra group membuka lowongan kerja. Lowongan kerja segera di buka untuk umum fresh graduate ataupun ...
 berpengalaman.

Kami membuka kesempatan yang sama, baik untuk para talenta muda dan juga untuk para profesional. Segera Pilih kategori yang sesuai dengan Skill/Jurusan atau pengalaman kerjamu!

LOWONGAN KERJA 2022

||LOWONGAN KERJA PABRIK TERBARU || LOKER SMA/SMK SEDERAJAT ||INFO LOWONGAN KERJA ASTRA GROUP TBK

POSISI LOWONGAN YG DIBUKA :
<H4>
OPERATOR PRODUKSI</H4>
<ul>
<li>Mengoperasikan, menjaga dan memberhentikan mesin produksi</li>
<li>Melakukan autonomous maintenance mesin</li>
<li>Membuat laporan monitoring proses produksi</li>
<li>Melakukan kontrol GMP dan standar produksi</li>
<li>Bertanggung jawab, rajin dan disiplin</li>
<li>Komunikatif dan mampu bekerjasama dengan baik</li>
</ul><H4>
STAFF ADMINISTRASI</H4>
<ul>
<li>Mengumpulkan Data Produksi</li>
<li>Memasukan Data ke Komputer</li>
<li>Mengontrol Proses Produksi</li>
<li>Menyusun Jadwal Pekerja</li>
<li>Menghitung Bahan-Bahan Produksi</li>
<li>Mencatat Efektifitas Kerja Mesin</li>
<li>Menerima Permintaan atau Pesanan</li>
<li>Melakukan Retur Sisa Bahan Baku</li>
</ul><H4>
STAFF GUDANG</H4>
<ul>
<li>Mendata Barang.</li>
<li>Melakukan Penataan Barang.</li>
<li>Melakukan Pemeliharaan Barang.</li>
<li>Mendata Barang Untuk Distribusi.</li>
<li>Saling Berkoordinasi Dalam Satu Tim.</li>
<li>Menjaga Kebersihan dan Kerapian Gudang.</li>
<li>Mengecek Kualitas Barang.</li>
<li>Memastikan Keamanan Barang.</li>
</ul><H4>
QUALITY CONTROL</H4>
<ul>
<li>Memantau dan menguji perkembangan semua produk yang diproduksi oleh perusahaan.</li>
<li>Memverifikasi kualitas produk</li>
<li>Memonitor setiap proses yang terlibat dalam produksi produk.</li>
<li>Memastikan kualitas barang produksi</li>
</ul>
sesuai standar agar lulus pemeriksaan.
<li>Merekomendasikan pengolahan ulang produk-produk berkualitas rendah.</li>
<li>Melakukan dokumentasi inspeksi dan tes yang dilakukan pada produk dari sebuah perusahaan.</li>
<li>Membuat analisis catatan sejarah perangkat dan dokumentasi produk sebelumnya untuk referensi di masa mendatang.</li>
<li>Membuat Pembukuan Personal QC / QCA</li>

KUALIFIKASI UMUM :
<li>Pria/Wanita</li>
<li>Usia 18 – 23 tahun</li>
<li>Pendidikan minimal SMA/SMK sederajat</li>
<li>Fresh Graduate/Berpengalaman</li>
<li>Berkelakuan baik</li>
<li>Sehat jasmani dan Rohani</li>
<li>Tidak bertatto/bertindik</li>
<li>Mau belajar dan Cepat belajar hal baru</li>
<li>Terbuka untuk umum (Sesuai kriteria)</li>

PERSYARATAN :
<li>Surat lamaran Kerja (Tulis Tangan)</li>
<li>CV / Daftar Riwayat Hidup (Tulis Tangan)</li>
<li>Fc Ijazah/ SKL</li>
<li>Fc KTP (sudah elektrik)</li>
<li>Fc SKCK (yang masih berlaku)</li>
<li>Fc Kartu Keluarga</li>
<li>Pas Foto 3 x 4 dan 4 x 6 (background merah)</li>
<li>NPWP</li>
<li>Surat Pencari Kerja (yang masih Aktif/berlaku)</li>
<li>Dan Berkas pendukung lainnya</li>

PENEMPATAN :
<li>Tangerang</li>
<li>Jakarta</li>
<li>Karawang</li>
<li>Bekasi</li>
<li>Cikarang</li>

Bagi para pencari kerja yang berminat silahkan segera kirimkan data lamaran kerja atau segera daftar secara online.

Pelamar yang sesuai kualifikasi akan segera di panggil seleksi test dan interview kerja.

Pendaftaran Langsung Secara Online Klik Link Website Dibawah ini :

Link >> www.astra.group-career.com

NOTE :
<li>CALON KANDIDAT DIWAJIBKAN SUDAH MELAKUKAN VAKSIN MIN DOSIS PERTAMA</li>
<li>INFORMASI LOWONGAN KERJA SEGERA DI TUTUP SEWAKTU WAKTU JIKA KEBUTUHAN KARYAWAN PERUASAHAAN SUDAH TERCUKUPI.</li>
<li>WASPADA PENIPUAN YANG MENGATAS NAMAKAN PT ASTRA</li>
<H4>
WARNING OF FRAUDULENT RECRUITMENT PROCESSES ON BEHALF OF PT ASTRA</H4>
<ul>
<li>PT ASTRA GROUP TIDAK MEMUNGUT BIAYA.</li>
<li>LOWONGAN KERJA MASIH TERBUKA SELAMA INFORMASI LOWONGAN KERJA INI MASIH ADA DAN TAYANG.</li>
</ul>
Guna meningkatkan produksi maka bagi calon karyawan yang telah lulus seleksi segera di tempatkan kerja di bagian yang telah di tentukan. Saat ini penempatan kerja di antaranya di kawasan jakarta , bekasi. cikarang, karawang dan masih ada yang lainya.

Segera cek informasi lowongan kerja selengkapnya di : INFO LOKER

<li>Membuat analisis catatan sejarah perangkat dan dokumentasi produk sebelumnya untuk referensi di masa mendatang.</li>
<li>Membuat Pembukuan Personal QC / QCA</li>

KUALIFIKASI UMUM :
<li>Pria/Wanita</li>
<li>Usia 18 – 23 tahun</li>
<li>Pendidikan minimal SMA/SMK sederajat</li>
<li>Fresh Graduate/Berpengalaman</li>
<li>Berkelakuan baik</li>
<li>Sehat jasmani dan Rohani</li>
<li>Tidak bertatto/bertindik</li>
<li>Mau belajar dan Cepat belajar hal baru</li>
<li>Terbuka untuk umum (Sesuai kriteria)</li>

PERSYARATAN :
<li>Surat lamaran Kerja (Tulis Tangan)</li>
<li>CV / Daftar Riwayat Hidup (Tulis Tangan)</li>
<li>Fc Ijazah/ SKL</li>
<li>Fc KTP (sudah elektrik)</li>
<li>Fc SKCK (yang masih berlaku)</li>
<li>Fc Kartu Keluarga</li>
<li>Pas Foto 3 x 4 dan 4 x 6 (background merah)</li>
<li>NPWP</li>
<li>Surat Pencari Kerja (yang masih Aktif/berlaku)</li>
<li>Dan Berkas pendukung lainnya</li>

PENEMPATAN :
<li>Tangerang</li>
<li>Jakarta</li>
<li>Karawang</li>
<li>Bekasi</li>
<li>Cikarang</li>

</ul>
Guna meningkatkan produksi maka bagi calon karyawan yang telah lulus seleksi segera di tempatkan kerja di bagian yang telah di tentukan. Saat ini penempatan kerja di antaranya di kawasan jakarta , bekasi. cikarang, karawang dan masih ada yang lainya.

||LOWONGAN KERJA PABRIK TERBARU|| LOKER SMA/SMK SEDERAJAT ||INFO LOWONGAN KERJA ASTRA GROUP TBK

LOWONGAN KERJA 2022 – PT Astra Group merupakan salah Satu Perusahaan Di bidang otomotif roda dua Dan empat terkemuka di Indonesia, Perusahaan ini Berdiri Pada Tahun 1957 setelah itu Sudah Menjadi Perusahaan Populer.

Hingga Pada tahun 1990, perusahaan mengubah nama menjadi PT Astra International Tbk.

PT Astra Group saat ini bergerak di bidang otomotif yang memproduksi Spare Part otomotif dan Perakitan Kendaraan Astra.Saat ini beberapa perusahaan yang bernaung di Astra Group di antaranya adalah :
<li>PT. ADM (Astra Daihatsu Motor)</li>
<li>PT. Toyota Astra Motor</li>
<li>PT. Astra Honda Motor (AHM)</li>
<li>PT. GS Baterai</li>
<li>PT. Showa Indonesia,</li>
<li>PT. Aisan Nasmoco Industri Manufaktur Otomotif,</li>
<li>dan masih banyak yang lainnya</li>

Guna mengisi beberapa posisi/bagian yang kosong maka perusahaan Astra group membuka lowongan kerja. Lowongan kerja segera di buka untuk umum fresh graduate ataupun ...
 berpengalaman.

Kami membuka kesempatan yang sama, baik untuk para talenta muda dan juga untuk para profesional. Segera Pilih kategori yang sesuai dengan Skill/Jurusan atau pengalaman kerjamu!

LOWONGAN KERJA 2022

||LOWONGAN KERJA PABRIK TERBARU || LOKER SMA/SMK SEDERAJAT ||INFO LOWONGAN KERJA ASTRA GROUP TBK

POSISI LOWONGAN YG DIBUKA :
<H4>
OPERATOR PRODUKSI</H4>
<ul>
<li>Mengoperasikan, menjaga dan memberhentikan mesin produksi</li>
<li>Melakukan autonomous maintenance mesin</li>
<li>Membuat laporan monitoring proses produksi</li>
<li>Melakukan kontrol GMP dan standar produksi</li>
<li>Bertanggung jawab, rajin dan disiplin</li>
<li>Komunikatif dan mampu bekerjasama dengan baik</li>
</ul><H4>
STAFF ADMINISTRASI</H4>
<ul>
<li>Mengumpulkan Data Produksi</li>
<li>Memasukan Data ke Komputer</li>
<li>Mengontrol Proses Produksi</li>
<li>Menyusun Jadwal Pekerja</li>
<li>Menghitung Bahan-Bahan Produksi</li>
<li>Mencatat Efektifitas Kerja Mesin</li>
<li>Menerima Permintaan atau Pesanan</li>
<li>Melakukan Retur Sisa Bahan Baku</li>
</ul><H4>
STAFF GUDANG</H4>
<ul>
<li>Mendata Barang.</li>
<li>Melakukan Penataan Barang.</li>
<li>Melakukan Pemeliharaan Barang.</li>
<li>Mendata Barang Untuk Distribusi.</li>
<li>Saling Berkoordinasi Dalam Satu Tim.</li>
<li>Menjaga Kebersihan dan Kerapian Gudang.</li>
<li>Mengecek Kualitas Barang.</li>
<li>Memastikan Keamanan Barang.</li>
</ul><H4>
QUALITY CONTROL</H4>
<ul>
<li>Memantau dan menguji perkembangan semua produk yang diproduksi oleh perusahaan.</li>
<li>Memverifikasi kualitas produk</li>
<li>Memonitor setiap proses yang terlibat dalam produksi produk.</li>
<li>Memastikan kualitas barang produksi</li>
</ul>
sesuai standar agar lulus pemeriksaan.
<li>Merekomendasikan pengolahan ulang produk-produk berkualitas rendah.</li>
<li>Melakukan dokumentasi inspeksi dan tes yang dilakukan pada produk dari sebuah perusahaan.</li>
<li>Membuat analisis catatan sejarah perangkat dan dokumentasi produk sebelumnya untuk referensi di masa mendatang.</li>
<li>Membuat Pembukuan Personal QC / QCA</li>

KUALIFIKASI UMUM :
<li>Pria/Wanita</li>
<li>Usia 18 – 23 tahun</li>
<li>Pendidikan minimal SMA/SMK sederajat</li>
<li>Fresh Graduate/Berpengalaman</li>
<li>Berkelakuan baik</li>
<li>Sehat jasmani dan Rohani</li>
<li>Tidak bertatto/bertindik</li>
<li>Mau belajar dan Cepat belajar hal baru</li>
<li>Terbuka untuk umum (Sesuai kriteria)</li>

PERSYARATAN :
<li>Surat lamaran Kerja (Tulis Tangan)</li>
<li>CV / Daftar Riwayat Hidup (Tulis Tangan)</li>
<li>Fc Ijazah/ SKL</li>
<li>Fc KTP (sudah elektrik)</li>
<li>Fc SKCK (yang masih berlaku)</li>
<li>Fc Kartu Keluarga</li>
<li>Pas Foto 3 x 4 dan 4 x 6 (background merah)</li>
<li>NPWP</li>
<li>Surat Pencari Kerja (yang masih Aktif/berlaku)</li>
<li>Dan Berkas pendukung lainnya</li>

PENEMPATAN :
<li>Tangerang</li>
<li>Jakarta</li>

<li>Bekasi</li>
<li>Cikarang</li>

<description><![CDATA[<div class="separator"><div style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img alt='Lowongan Kerja Terbaru Dan Terupdate 2022 | FORUM HRD INDONESIA' src='https://encrypted-tbn0.gstatic.com/images?q=tbn:ANd9GcQ8m4zRj6Qcmc5yDRuJceBDmhGDb6_1H9N02spl2STR8g&usqp=CAU&ec=48665701' width='640' height='239' /></div></div><br /><br /><br /><b>LOWONGAN KERJA 2023 PT EPSON INDONESIA | KARYAWAN PABRIK ELEKTRONIK PT. INDONESIA EPSON INDUSTRY   Cikedokan, Kabupaten Bekasi, Jawa Barat   </b>  <h3>Overview:</h3> <blockquote><i>Pekerjaan tetap<br/> PT. INDONESIA EPSON INDUSTRY<br/>  Cikedokan, Kabupaten Bekasi, Jawa Barat   </i></blockquote><h3>Responsibilities:</h3> <div class"jobresponsibilities"> </div><br /><div class="separator"><div style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img alt='Lowongan Kerja: Indonesia — 32.000+ Lowongan Kerja Terbaru — Jooble' src='https://encrypted-tbn0.gstatic.com/images?q=tbn:ANd9GcQO01T6lsBA7vRrTUBD7F5NAT90_VhRhfdWZA&usqp=CAU' width='640' height='256' /></div></div><br /><br /><br /> <h3>Job Description:</h3> <div class"jobdescription">PT INDONESIA EPSON INDUSTRY merupakan salah satu perusahaan yang bergerak dalam pengolahan komponen Elektronik terkemuka di Indonesia, Perusahaan ini berdiri pada tahun 1942 setelah itu sudah menjadi perusahaan populer. Dan selanjutnya membuktikan dirinya sebagai salah satu produsen elektronik berkualitas tinggi dan telah banyak mendapatkan penghargaan.

PT Indonesia EPSON Industry mempunyai karyawan lebih dari 10.000 dan menghasilkan 1 juta printer dalam 1 bulan, sedangkan beberapa produk dari EPSON yang tentu sudah tidak asing lagi ditemui selama ini diantaranya adalah Printer, Injector, Projector dan masih banyak yang lainnya.

Saat ini pihak manajemen membuka kesempatan bagi putra-putri bangsa untuk memperkembang kan karir bersama PT Indonesia Epson Industry untuk menempati posisi dengan kualifikasi sebagai berikut

LOWONGAN KERJA TERBARU PT INDONESIA EPSON INDUSTRY

Posisi Yang Terbuka Saat ini :
<li>Operator Produksi</li>
<li>Operator Assembling</li>
<li>Operator Quality Control</li>
<li>Staff ...</li>
<H4> Administrasi</H4>
<ul>
<li>Staff Gudang</li>
</ul>
Kualifikasi Umum :
<li>Pendidikan Minimal SMA/SMK Sederajat</li>
<li>Pria dan Wanita</li>
<li>Range umur 18 Tahun – maksimal 25 Tahun</li>

Kriteria Fisik :
<li>Pria Tinggi badan minimal 160 Cm</li>
<li>Wanita Tinggi badan minimal 150 Cm</li>
<li>Wanita memiliki tindik Telinga Sepasang</li>
<li>Tidak memiliki Tatto</li>
<li>Tidak memiliki Fisik Cacat</li>

Cara Melamar :

Apabila Anda Memenuhi Kualifikasi di Atas, Silahkan Kirim Pengajuan Data Singkat Anda Kebagian Penyelenggaraan Recruitment dan Seleksi Perusahaan PT Indonesia Epson Industry via online Dengan dengan cara daftar pada format di bawah ini :

# PENEMPATAN KERJA SURABAYA, SIDOARJO DAN GRESIK #

GAJI ±4,500.000 jt / bln

Dll

<title>Lowongan Kerja Karyawan Pabrik Area Purwakarta Juni 2022 Pt. Omron Manufacturing Of Indonesia   Nagri Kidul, Kabupaten Purwakarta, Jawa Barat   </title>
<pubDate>Fri, 28 Apr 2023 17:29:18 +0000</pubDate>
<dc:creator>Freelance</dc:creator>
<guid isPermaLink="true">None</guid>
<description><![CDATA[<div class="separator"><div style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img alt='PT Kereta Api Pariwisata Buka Lowongan Kerja di Banyak Kota, Simak  Persyaratannya Halaman all - Kompas.com' src='https://encrypted-tbn0.gstatic.com/images?q=tbn:ANd9GcQKt5OWgUE5_ISzMQAUVlxLIROG9LPiLNFhyMhGpGVtpw&usqp=CAU&ec=48665698' width='640' height='320' /></div></div><br /><br /><br /><b>Lowongan Kerja Karyawan Pabrik Area Purwakarta Juni 2022 PT. Omron Manufacturing of Indonesia   Nagri Kidul, Kabupaten Purwakarta, Jawa Barat   </b>  <h3>Overview:</h3> <blockquote><i>Pekerjaan tetap<br/> PT. Omron Manufacturing of Indonesia<br/>  Nagri Kidul, Kabupaten Purwakarta, Jawa Barat   </i></blockquote><h3>Responsibilities:</h3> <div class"jobresponsibilities"> </div><br /><div class="separator"><div style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img alt='Lowongan Kerja PT Linknet,Tbk FIRST MEDIA Bandung & Purwakarta April 2022 -  Info Loker Bandung Terbaru 2023' src='https://encrypted-tbn0.gstatic.com/images?q=tbn:ANd9GcRTXDEJXkoWG-CIDC6qz89aZQUSr3fNeiuy_nVXbn8n9Q&usqp=CAU&ec=48665698' width='640' height='359' /></div></div><br /><br /><br /> <h3>Job Description:</h3> <div class"jobdescription">Lowongan Kerja Terbaru Cikarang 2022, Info Loker Terbaru hari Ini, Lowongan Kerja Lulusan SMA SMK D3 S1, Loker terbaru Via Email, Info Loker Terbaru Via Online, Loker Operator Produksi, Lowongan kerja Terbaru 2022

Lowongan Kerja Karyawan Pabrik Area Purwakarta Juni 2022 – PT Omron Manufacturing of Indonesia merupakan salah satu cabang dari perusahaan elektronik asal Jepang yaitu Omron Corp Jepang yang terdepan dan terkemuka dalam Industri sistem kontrol otomasi yang berlokasi di EJIP Industrial Park, Cikarang, Bekasi, Jawa Barat.

PT Omron Manufacturing of Indonesia sebagai produsen global untuk Relay dan Switch telah lebih dari 25 tahun beroperasi di Indonesia dan terus tumbuh dan berkembang dengan mendirikan pabrik otomasi yang memproduksi Sensor, Counter dan Timer serta memberikan solusi bisnis secara menyeluruh untuk Otomasi Industri.

Lowongan Kerja Karyawan Pabrik Area Purwakarta Juni 2022

Posisi :
<li>Operator Produksi</li>
<li>Quality Control</li>
<li>Staff Admin</li>
<li>Assembling</li>

Kualifikasi ...
 :
<li>Usia minimal 18 tahun maksimal 28 tahun</li>
<li>Memiliki latar belakang pendidikan SMA/SMK semua jurusan</li>
<li>Bebas Narkoba dan memiliki SKCK</li>
<li>Sehat jasmani dan rohani dibuktikan dengan surat dokter</li>
<li>Siap di tempatkan di cikarang bekasi</li>

Apabila kalian berminat dengan lowongan PT Omron Mfg indonesia diatas, Silahkan Apply For Job via Online dibawah ini :

Alamat PT Omron Manufacturing of Indonesia

Kawasan Industri EJIP Plot 5C Sukaresmi, Cikarang Selatan Bekasi 17550

Lowongan Kerja Karyawan Pabrik Area Purwakarta Juni 2022 – PT Omron Manufacturing of Indonesia merupakan salah satu cabang dari perusahaan elektronik asal Jepang yaitu Omron Corp Jepang yang terdepan dan terkemuka dalam Industri sistem kontrol otomasi yang berlokasi di EJIP Industrial Park, Cikarang, Bekasi, Jawa Barat.

PT Omron Manufacturing of Indonesia sebagai produsen global untuk Relay dan Switch telah lebih dari 25 tahun beroperasi di Indonesia dan terus tumbuh dan berkembang dengan mendirikan pabrik otomasi yang memproduksi Sensor, Counter dan Timer serta memberikan solusi bisnis secara menyeluruh untuk Otomasi Industri.

Lowongan Kerja Karyawan Pabrik Area Purwakarta Juni 2022

Posisi :
<li>Operator Produksi</li>
<li>Quality Control</li>
<li>Staff Admin</li>
<li>Assembling</li>

Kualifikasi ...
 :
<li>Usia minimal 18 tahun maksimal 28 tahun</li>
<li>Memiliki latar belakang pendidikan SMA/SMK semua jurusan</li>
<li>Bebas Narkoba dan memiliki SKCK</li>
<li>Sehat jasmani dan rohani dibuktikan dengan surat dokter</li>
<li>Siap di tempatkan di cikarang bekasi</li>

Apabila kalian berminat dengan lowongan PT Omron Mfg indonesia diatas, Silahkan Apply For Job via Online dibawah ini :

Alamat PT Omron Manufacturing of Indonesia

Kawasan Industri EJIP Plot 5C Sukaresmi, Cikarang Selatan Bekasi 17550

<title>Pt Yamaha Indonesia Motor Manufacturing – Daftar Lowongan Kerja... Pt Yamaha Indonesia Motor Mfg Karir   Kabupaten Garut, Jawa Barat   </title>
<pubDate>Mon, 01 May 2023 16:30:06 +0000</pubDate>
<dc:creator>Freelance</dc:creator>
<guid isPermaLink="true">None</guid>
<description><![CDATA[<div class="separator"><div style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img alt='Lowongan Kerja Operator Produksi PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Manufacturing  2022 – Lokerja.info' src='https://encrypted-tbn0.gstatic.com/images?q=tbn:ANd9GcQNd7uuv1qAPT29mEd7l4ECFxRgbkMnjFEVM51hdWU5Qg&usqp=CAU&ec=48600112' width='640' height='377' /></div></div><br /><br /><br /><b>PT YAMAHA INDONESIA MOTOR MANUFACTURING – DAFTAR LOWONGAN KERJA... PT YAMAHA INDONESIA MOTOR MFG KARIR   Kabupaten Garut, Jawa Barat   </b>  <h3>Overview:</h3> <blockquote><i>Kontraktor
Rp 8,5 jt per bulan<br/> PT YAMAHA INDONESIA MOTOR MFG KARIR<br/>  Kabupaten Garut, Jawa Barat   </i></blockquote><h3>Responsibilities:</h3> <div class"jobresponsibilities"> </div><br /><div class="separator"><div style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img alt='Lowongan Kerja PT. Yamaha Indonesia Motor Manufacturing Februari 2021' src='https://encrypted-tbn0.gstatic.com/images?q=tbn:ANd9GcSdVFRJxDIpfYWEJsRN7e61uvhmdY83uBU0gXWhYkmYQQ&usqp=CAU&ec=48600112' width='640' height='242' /></div></div><br /><br /><br /> <h3>Job Description:</h3> <div class"jobdescription">FORUMHRDINDONESIA.COM | PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Manufacturing atau lebih dikenal dengan PT YIMM adalah salah satu perusahaan yang bergerak dalam industri perakitan kendaraan, terutama kendaraan roda 2.

Group bisnis Yamaha Indonesia merupakan perusahaan PMA asal Jepang yang telah memulai bisnis perakitan kendaraan di Indonesia sejak tahun 1974.

PT YIMM selaku Agen Tunggal Pemegang Merek (ATPM) Yamaha di Indonesia merupakan pihak yang berwenang atas produk roda dua Yamaha di Indonesia.

PT YIMM memproduksi kendaraan roda dua dan dipasarkan dengan merek dagang Yamaha.

Selain itu, Yamaha Group juga memproduksi serta memasarkan suku cadang dan aksesoris kendaraan.

Beberapa produk sepeda motor yang diproduksi oleh PT YIMM diantaranya Yamaha Mio, Fino, NMAX, Aerox, YZF R15, dan masih banyak lainnya

Guna meningkatkan kinerja dan produktifitas perusahaan yang lebih baik, pihak manajemen membuka kesempatan bagi putra-putri bangsa untuk bergabung dalam lowongan kerja PT Yamaha Indonesia ...
 Motor Mfg untuk menempati posisi dengan kualifikasi sebagai berikut :

Posisi Yang Terbuka Yakini :
<li>Operator Produksi Manufacturing</li>
<li>Operator Assembling/Perakitan</li>
<li>Operator QC (Quality Control)</li>
<li>Staff Administrasi</li>

Persyaratan Sebagai Operator Produksi :
<li>Pria/Wanita</li>
<li>Usia 18 – 20 tahun</li>
<li>Pendidikan minimal SMA/SMK sederajat diutamakan jurusan Teknik Mesin/Otomotif/Elektro/Listrik</li>
<li>Nilai rata-rata rapor minimal 6</li>
<li>Belum pernah menikah dan tidak sedang hamil</li>
<li>Sebelumnya tidak pernah bekerja di PT. Yamaha Indonesia Motor Mfg</li>
<li>Lulusan 3 tahun terakhir dan tidak sedang menjalani perkuliahan</li>

Kriteria Fisik :
<li>Tinggi badan minimal Pria 160 cm, Wanita 158 cm dengan berat badan ideal</li>
<li>Tidak minus/plus/buta warna</li>
<li>Tidak bertato dan tidak bertindik</li>
<li>Untuk wanita tindik maksimal 1 pasang</li>
<li>Tidak ada cacat tubuh</li>
<li>Rambut rapi, khusus Pria panjang rambut maksimal 2 cm</li>

Persyaratan Umum :
<li>Laki-laki / Perempuan</li>
<li>Pendidikan minimal SMA/SMK sederajat diutamakan jurusan Teknik Mesin/Otomotif/Elektro/Listrik</li>
<li>Usia 18 tahun – 24 tahun</li>
<li>Sehat dan tidak buta warna</li>
<li>Bersedia bekerja shift dan lembur</li>
<li>Fresh Graduate lebih diutamakan</li>
<li>Penempatan Area Jakarta Bekasi Karawang</li>

Kriteria Sikap & Perilaku :

Memiliki semangat untuk bekerja, mau belajar, mampu bekerja di bawah tekanan, bersedia untuk bekerja lembur dan atau shift , sopan, jujur, tidak emosional .Tidak pernah terlibat narkoba, minuman keras, tindak kriminal, dan asusila

Cara Melamar Kerja di PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Mfg (YIMM) Terbaru Tahun 2021 :

Apabila Saudari memenuhi kualifikasi PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Mfg (YIMM) tersebut, Saudari bisa melamar ke yayasan penyalur kerja yang bekerjasama dengan PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Mfg (YIMM) / Mengajukan Pendaftaran Online PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Mfg (YIMM)

PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Manufacturing (YIMM)

Link Pendaftaran Online : https://www.forumhrdindonesia.com/yamaha-job-apply/

Deadline lowongan tidak ditentukan dan dapat ditutup sewaktu-waktu apabila kuota penerimaan karyawan telah mencukupi pada tahun 2021

Hanya calon tenaga kerja yang dapat memenuhi kualifikasi yang akan dipanggil untuk mengikuti seleksi dan wawancara kerja.

Information :
<li>Proses seleksi Dan Recruitment di Tentukan oleh Tim Seleksi Global Development Center PT. Yamaha Indonesia Motor Mfg di Bekasi</li>
<li>Bukan Yayasan Atau Outcorsing</li>
<li>Panggilan Tes tidak bisa di ganggu gugat (Hanya yang memenuhi Syarat yang akan di Proses)</li>

PT YAMAHA INDONESIA MOTOR MFG TIDAK PERNAH MEMUNGUT BIAYA APAPUN TERHADAP CALON PELAMAR

Sumber Resmi https://yamaha-motor.co.id/career/

PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Manufacturing

Alamat : Jl. DR. KRT. Rajiman Widyodiningrat – Jl. Raya Bekasi Km 23 Pulo Gadung – Jakarta 13920

PT. Yamaha Indonesia Motor Manufacturing West Java Factory (Plant 2)

Alamat: Kawasan Industri KIIC, Jl. Permata I Lot BB 1, Puseurjaya, Telukjambe Timur, Puseurjaya, Kec. Telukjambe Tim., Kabupaten Karawang, Jawa Barat 41361

Note :

<li>Proses seleksi peserta di PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Manufacturing termasuk cepat, LAMARAN akan diperlakukan secara rahasia & hanya kandidat terpilih akan dihubungi dan diproses</li>

<li>Jika lolos maka anda akan langsung masuk tahap selanjutnya.</li>

<content:encoded><![CDATA[<div class="separator"><div style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img alt='Lowongan Kerja Operator Produksi PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Manufacturing  2022 – Lokerja.info' src='https://encrypted-tbn0.gstatic.com/images?q=tbn:ANd9GcQNd7uuv1qAPT29mEd7l4ECFxRgbkMnjFEVM51hdWU5Qg&usqp=CAU&ec=48600112' width='640' height='377' /></div></div><br /><br /><br /><b>PT YAMAHA INDONESIA MOTOR MANUFACTURING – DAFTAR LOWONGAN KERJA... PT YAMAHA INDONESIA MOTOR MFG KARIR   Kabupaten Garut, Jawa Barat   </b>  <h3>Overview:</h3> <blockquote><i>Kontraktor
Rp 8,5 jt per bulan<br/> PT YAMAHA INDONESIA MOTOR MFG KARIR<br/>  Kabupaten Garut, Jawa Barat   </i></blockquote><h3>Responsibilities:</h3> <div class"jobresponsibilities"> </div><br /><div class="separator"><div style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img alt='Lowongan Kerja PT. Yamaha Indonesia Motor Manufacturing Februari 2021' src='https://encrypted-tbn0.gstatic.com/images?q=tbn:ANd9GcSdVFRJxDIpfYWEJsRN7e61uvhmdY83uBU0gXWhYkmYQQ&usqp=CAU&ec=48600112' width='640' height='242' /></div></div><br /><br /><br /> <h3>Job Description:</h3> <div class"jobdescription">FORUMHRDINDONESIA.COM | PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Manufacturing atau lebih dikenal dengan PT YIMM adalah salah satu perusahaan yang bergerak dalam industri perakitan kendaraan, terutama kendaraan roda 2.

Group bisnis Yamaha Indonesia merupakan perusahaan PMA asal Jepang yang telah memulai bisnis perakitan kendaraan di Indonesia sejak tahun 1974.

PT YIMM selaku Agen Tunggal Pemegang Merek (ATPM) Yamaha di Indonesia merupakan pihak yang berwenang atas produk roda dua Yamaha di Indonesia.

PT YIMM memproduksi kendaraan roda dua dan dipasarkan dengan merek dagang Yamaha.

Selain itu, Yamaha Group juga memproduksi serta memasarkan suku cadang dan aksesoris kendaraan.

Beberapa produk sepeda motor yang diproduksi oleh PT YIMM diantaranya Yamaha Mio, Fino, NMAX, Aerox, YZF R15, dan masih banyak lainnya

Guna meningkatkan kinerja dan produktifitas perusahaan yang lebih baik, pihak manajemen membuka kesempatan bagi putra-putri bangsa untuk bergabung dalam lowongan kerja PT Yamaha Indonesia ...
 Motor Mfg untuk menempati posisi dengan kualifikasi sebagai berikut :

Posisi Yang Terbuka Yakini :
<li>Operator Produksi Manufacturing</li>
<li>Operator Assembling/Perakitan</li>
<li>Operator QC (Quality Control)</li>
<li>Staff Administrasi</li>

Persyaratan Sebagai Operator Produksi :
<li>Pria/Wanita</li>
<li>Usia 18 – 20 tahun</li>
<li>Pendidikan minimal SMA/SMK sederajat diutamakan jurusan Teknik Mesin/Otomotif/Elektro/Listrik</li>
<li>Nilai rata-rata rapor minimal 6</li>
<li>Belum pernah menikah dan tidak sedang hamil</li>
<li>Sebelumnya tidak pernah bekerja di PT. Yamaha Indonesia Motor Mfg</li>
<li>Lulusan 3 tahun terakhir dan tidak sedang menjalani perkuliahan</li>

Kriteria Fisik :
<li>Tinggi badan minimal Pria 160 cm, Wanita 158 cm dengan berat badan ideal</li>
<li>Tidak minus/plus/buta warna</li>
<li>Tidak bertato dan tidak bertindik</li>
<li>Untuk wanita tindik maksimal 1 pasang</li>
<li>Tidak ada cacat tubuh</li>
<li>Rambut rapi, khusus Pria panjang rambut maksimal 2 cm</li>

Persyaratan Umum :
<li>Laki-laki / Perempuan</li>
<li>Pendidikan minimal SMA/SMK sederajat diutamakan jurusan Teknik Mesin/Otomotif/Elektro/Listrik</li>
<li>Usia 18 tahun – 24 tahun</li>
<li>Sehat dan tidak buta warna</li>
<li>Bersedia bekerja shift dan lembur</li>
<li>Fresh Graduate lebih diutamakan</li>
<li>Penempatan Area Jakarta Bekasi Karawang</li>

Kriteria Sikap & Perilaku :

Memiliki semangat untuk bekerja, mau belajar, mampu bekerja di bawah tekanan, bersedia untuk bekerja lembur dan atau shift , sopan, jujur, tidak emosional .Tidak pernah terlibat narkoba, minuman keras, tindak kriminal, dan asusila

Cara Melamar Kerja di PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Mfg (YIMM) Terbaru Tahun 2021 :

Apabila Saudari memenuhi kualifikasi PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Mfg (YIMM) tersebut, Saudari bisa melamar ke yayasan penyalur kerja yang bekerjasama dengan PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Mfg (YIMM) / Mengajukan Pendaftaran Online PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Mfg (YIMM)

PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Manufacturing (YIMM)

Link Pendaftaran Online : https://www.forumhrdindonesia.com/yamaha-job-apply/

Deadline lowongan tidak ditentukan dan dapat ditutup sewaktu-waktu apabila kuota penerimaan karyawan telah mencukupi pada tahun 2021

Hanya calon tenaga kerja yang dapat memenuhi kualifikasi yang akan dipanggil untuk mengikuti seleksi dan wawancara kerja.

Information :
<li>Proses seleksi Dan Recruitment di Tentukan oleh Tim Seleksi Global Development Center PT. Yamaha Indonesia Motor Mfg di Bekasi</li>
<li>Bukan Yayasan Atau Outcorsing</li>
<li>Panggilan Tes tidak bisa di ganggu gugat (Hanya yang memenuhi Syarat yang akan di Proses)</li>

PT YAMAHA INDONESIA MOTOR MFG TIDAK PERNAH MEMUNGUT BIAYA APAPUN TERHADAP CALON PELAMAR

Sumber Resmi https://yamaha-motor.co.id/career/

PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Manufacturing

Alamat : Jl. DR. KRT. Rajiman Widyodiningrat – Jl. Raya Bekasi Km 23 Pulo Gadung – Jakarta 13920

PT. Yamaha Indonesia Motor Manufacturing West Java Factory (Plant 2)

Alamat: Kawasan Industri KIIC, Jl. Permata I Lot BB 1, Puseurjaya, Telukjambe Timur, Puseurjaya, Kec. Telukjambe Tim., Kabupaten Karawang, Jawa Barat 41361

Note :

<li>Proses seleksi peserta di PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Manufacturing termasuk cepat, LAMARAN akan diperlakukan secara rahasia & hanya kandidat terpilih akan dihubungi dan diproses</li>

<li>Jika lolos maka anda akan langsung masuk tahap selanjutnya.</li>

Demikian informasi lowongan kerja yang kami berikan hari ini,semoga bermanfaat dan dapat membantu anda yang sedang mencari pekerjaan.

<excerpt:encoded><![CDATA[<div class="separator"><div style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img alt='Lowongan Kerja Operator Produksi PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Manufacturing  2022 – Lokerja.info' src='https://encrypted-tbn0.gstatic.com/images?q=tbn:ANd9GcQNd7uuv1qAPT29mEd7l4ECFxRgbkMnjFEVM51hdWU5Qg&usqp=CAU&ec=48600112' width='640' height='377' /></div></div><br /><br /><br /><b>PT YAMAHA INDONESIA MOTOR MANUFACTURING – DAFTAR LOWONGAN KERJA... PT YAMAHA INDONESIA MOTOR MFG KARIR   Kabupaten Garut, Jawa Barat   </b>  <h3>Overview:</h3> <blockquote><i>Kontraktor
Rp 8,5 jt per bulan<br/> PT YAMAHA INDONESIA MOTOR MFG KARIR<br/>  Kabupaten Garut, Jawa Barat   </i></blockquote><h3>Responsibilities:</h3> <div class"jobresponsibilities"> </div><br /><div class="separator"><div style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img alt='Lowongan Kerja PT. Yamaha Indonesia Motor Manufacturing Februari 2021' src='https://encrypted-tbn0.gstatic.com/images?q=tbn:ANd9GcSdVFRJxDIpfYWEJsRN7e61uvhmdY83uBU0gXWhYkmYQQ&usqp=CAU&ec=48600112' width='640' height='242' /></div></div><br /><br /><br /> <h3>Job Description:</h3> <div class"jobdescription">FORUMHRDINDONESIA.COM | PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Manufacturing atau lebih dikenal dengan PT YIMM adalah salah satu perusahaan yang bergerak dalam industri perakitan kendaraan, terutama kendaraan roda 2.

Group bisnis Yamaha Indonesia merupakan perusahaan PMA asal Jepang yang telah memulai bisnis perakitan kendaraan di Indonesia sejak tahun 1974.

PT YIMM selaku Agen Tunggal Pemegang Merek (ATPM) Yamaha di Indonesia merupakan pihak yang berwenang atas produk roda dua Yamaha di Indonesia.

PT YIMM memproduksi kendaraan roda dua dan dipasarkan dengan merek dagang Yamaha.

Selain itu, Yamaha Group juga memproduksi serta memasarkan suku cadang dan aksesoris kendaraan.

Beberapa produk sepeda motor yang diproduksi oleh PT YIMM diantaranya Yamaha Mio, Fino, NMAX, Aerox, YZF R15, dan masih banyak lainnya

Guna meningkatkan kinerja dan produktifitas perusahaan yang lebih baik, pihak manajemen membuka kesempatan bagi putra-putri bangsa untuk bergabung dalam lowongan kerja PT Yamaha Indonesia ...
 Motor Mfg untuk menempati posisi dengan kualifikasi sebagai berikut :

Posisi Yang Terbuka Yakini :
<li>Operator Produksi Manufacturing</li>
<li>Operator Assembling/Perakitan</li>
<li>Operator QC (Quality Control)</li>
<li>Staff Administrasi</li>

Persyaratan Sebagai Operator Produksi :
<li>Pria/Wanita</li>
<li>Usia 18 – 20 tahun</li>
<li>Pendidikan minimal SMA/SMK sederajat diutamakan jurusan Teknik Mesin/Otomotif/Elektro/Listrik</li>
<li>Nilai rata-rata rapor minimal 6</li>
<li>Belum pernah menikah dan tidak sedang hamil</li>
<li>Sebelumnya tidak pernah bekerja di PT. Yamaha Indonesia Motor Mfg</li>
<li>Lulusan 3 tahun terakhir dan tidak sedang menjalani perkuliahan</li>

Kriteria Fisik :
<li>Tinggi badan minimal Pria 160 cm, Wanita 158 cm dengan berat badan ideal</li>
<li>Tidak minus/plus/buta warna</li>
<li>Tidak bertato dan tidak bertindik</li>
<li>Untuk wanita tindik maksimal 1 pasang</li>
<li>Tidak ada cacat tubuh</li>
<li>Rambut rapi, khusus Pria panjang rambut maksimal 2 cm</li>

Persyaratan Umum :
<li>Laki-laki / Perempuan</li>
<li>Pendidikan minimal SMA/SMK sederajat diutamakan jurusan Teknik Mesin/Otomotif/Elektro/Listrik</li>
<li>Usia 18 tahun – 24 tahun</li>
<li>Sehat dan tidak buta warna</li>
<li>Bersedia bekerja shift dan lembur</li>
<li>Fresh Graduate lebih diutamakan</li>
<li>Penempatan Area Jakarta Bekasi Karawang</li>

Kriteria Sikap & Perilaku :

Memiliki semangat untuk bekerja, mau belajar, mampu bekerja di bawah tekanan, bersedia untuk bekerja lembur dan atau shift , sopan, jujur, tidak emosional .Tidak pernah terlibat narkoba, minuman keras, tindak kriminal, dan asusila

Cara Melamar Kerja di PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Mfg (YIMM) Terbaru Tahun 2021 :

Apabila Saudari memenuhi kualifikasi PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Mfg (YIMM) tersebut, Saudari bisa melamar ke yayasan penyalur kerja yang bekerjasama dengan PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Mfg (YIMM) / Mengajukan Pendaftaran Online PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Mfg (YIMM)

PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Manufacturing (YIMM)

Link Pendaftaran Online : https://www.forumhrdindonesia.com/yamaha-job-apply/

Deadline lowongan tidak ditentukan dan dapat ditutup sewaktu-waktu apabila kuota penerimaan karyawan telah mencukupi pada tahun 2021

Hanya calon tenaga kerja yang dapat memenuhi kualifikasi yang akan dipanggil untuk mengikuti seleksi dan wawancara kerja.

Information :
<li>Proses seleksi Dan Recruitment di Tentukan oleh Tim Seleksi Global Development Center PT. Yamaha Indonesia Motor Mfg di Bekasi</li>
<li>Bukan Yayasan Atau Outcorsing</li>
<li>Panggilan Tes tidak bisa di ganggu gugat (Hanya yang memenuhi Syarat yang akan di Proses)</li>

PT YAMAHA INDONESIA MOTOR MFG TIDAK PERNAH MEMUNGUT BIAYA APAPUN TERHADAP CALON PELAMAR

Sumber Resmi https://yamaha-motor.co.id/career/

PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Manufacturing

Alamat : Jl. DR. KRT. Rajiman Widyodiningrat – Jl. Raya Bekasi Km 23 Pulo Gadung – Jakarta 13920

PT. Yamaha Indonesia Motor Manufacturing West Java Factory (Plant 2)

Alamat: Kawasan Industri KIIC, Jl. Permata I Lot BB 1, Puseurjaya, Telukjambe Timur, Puseurjaya, Kec. Telukjambe Tim., Kabupaten Karawang, Jawa Barat 41361

Note :

<li>Proses seleksi peserta di PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Manufacturing termasuk cepat, LAMARAN akan diperlakukan secara rahasia & hanya kandidat terpilih akan dihubungi dan diproses</li>

<li>Jika lolos maka anda akan langsung masuk tahap selanjutnya.</li>

Demikian informasi lowongan kerja yang kami berikan hari ini,semoga bermanfaat dan dapat membantu anda yang sedang mencari pekerjaan.

INFO LOKER BARU | LOWONGAN KERJA PABRIK

PT YAMAHA INDONESIA MOTOR MFG

LOWONGAN KERJA 2023 | Yamaha Group memproduksi kendaraan roda dua dan dipasarkan dengan merek dagang Yamaha.

PT YAMAHA INDONESIA MOTOR MFG berhasil memproduksi serta memasarkan suku cadang dan aksesoris kendaraan.

Hasil produk sepeda motor yang diproduksi oleh PT YIMM adalah Yamaha Mio, Fino, NMAX, Aerox, YZF R15, dan masih banyak lainnya

Guna meningkatkan kinerja dan produktifitas perusahaan yang lebih baik maka pihak manajemen membuka peluang kerja bagi putra-putri bangsa untuk segera bergabung dalam lowongan kerja PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Manufacturing untuk menempati posisi sesuai kebutuhan perusahaan.

Dibutuhkan :
<li>Operator produksi</li>
<li>Operator Gudang</li>
<li>Staff Admin</li>

Kualifikasi Umum :
<li>Usia 18 – 22 Tahun</li>
<li>Pendidikan SMA/SMK/MA atau sederajat</li>
<li>Belum pernah bekerja di PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Manufacturing</li>
<li>Belum pernah menikah</li>
<li>Tidak sedang kuliah</li>
<li>Berbadan ...</li>
 sehat, bebas Covid-19 dibuktikan dengan Surat Keterangan Hasil Rapid Test Antigen Covid-19 dari Klinik/Rumah Sakit
<li>Sudah melakukan vaksin Covid-19 minimal dosis 2 (diutamakan sudah vaksin Booster) dibuktikan dengan Sertifikat Vaksin Covid-19</li>
<li>Tidak pernah terlibat dalam penyalahgunaan narkotika/obat terlarang dan minuman keras</li>

Persyaratan :
<li>Surat lamaran kerja</li>
<li>Daftar riwayat hidup</li>
<li>Fc. ijazah/SKL</li>
<li>Fc. ktp</li>
<li>Fc. Kartu vaksin</li>
<li>Fc kartu keluarga</li>
<li>Fc. SKCK (Yang masih aktif/hidup)</li>
<li>Dan berkas pendukung lainnya.</li>

Fasilitas :
<li>Gaji</li>
<li>seragam</li>
<li>BPJS</li>
<li>Lembur</li>
<li>Jemputan</li>
<li>Dan lain lain</li>

Penempatan Area :
<li>Jakarta</li>
<li>Cikarang</li>
<li>Karawang</li>

LOWONGAN KERJA 2023 | INFO LOWONGAN KERJA

Calon pelamar yang Berminat segera melakukan Pendaftaran secara Online melalui link yang sudah di sediakan oleh perusahaan atau langsung daftar ke Yayasan/ LPTKS atau BKK Yang di percaya/ di tunjuk oleh perusahaan.

Segera Klik Link Dan lengkapi data guna melakukan Pendaftaran :

Applyjobs/career/sma-smk

Bagi pelamar yang sesuai kualifikasi akan segera di panggil melakukan seleksi beserta walk interview.Silakan baca dan cermati dengan semua kriteria yang kami cari sehingga bisa mengikuti seleksi menjadi karyawan di Perusahaan ini.

Sesuaikan kualifikasi diri Anda dengan kriteria tersebut sehingga Anda bisa mengikuti proses seleksi calon pekerja PT YIMM.

Lowongan kerja untuk Operator Produksi dan yang terkait langsung dengan proses produksi dan mesin produksi.

Sehingga tercukupi kebutuhan man power untuk bagian operator produksi dan non produksi (Contoh: bagian logistik dan bagian fasilitas).

Calon karyawan yang lulus seleksi akan segera mendapatkan penempatan kerja sesuai kebutuhan perusahaan.

Bagi karyawan yang kinerja nya bagus ada jenjang karir sehingga bisa menjadi karyawan tetap.

Informasi lowongan kerja selengkapnya segera klik dan cek : INFO LOKER

ALAMAT PERUSAHAAN :
<li>PT YIMM ( PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Manufacturing ) Jl. DR. KRT. Rajiman Widyodiningrat KM. 23, RT.10/RW.4, Rawa Terate, Cakung, Kota Jakarta Timur, Daerah Khusus Ibukota Jakarta 13920</li>
<li>PT YMMWJ ( PT Yamaha Motor Manufacturing West Java ) Kawasan Industri KIIC, Jl. Permata I Lot BB 1, Puseurjaya, Telukjambe Timur, Puseurjaya, Kec. Telukjambe Tim., Kabupaten Karawang, Jawa Barat 41361</li>
<li>PT YPMI ( PT Yamaha Motor Parts Manufacturing Indonesia ) Kawasan Industri KIIC, Jl. Permata Raya Lot F2 Dan F6, Sukaluyu, Teluk Jambe Timur, Karawang, Jawa Barat 41361</li>

PT YAMAHA INDONESIA MOTOR MANUFACTURING (Bagian Divisi Operasional)
<li>Kawasan Industri MM 2100, Jl. Irian Blok HH No. 1, Jatiwangi, Kec. Cikarang Bar., Bekasi, Jawa Barat 17530</li>

Lowongan kerja bisa di tutup sewaktu waktu jika kebutuhan Karyawan baru di anggap sudah cukup.

PT YAMAHA INDONESIA MOTOR MFG

LOWONGAN KERJA 2023 | Yamaha Group memproduksi kendaraan roda dua dan dipasarkan dengan merek dagang Yamaha.

PT YAMAHA INDONESIA MOTOR MFG berhasil memproduksi serta memasarkan suku cadang dan aksesoris kendaraan.

Guna meningkatkan kinerja dan produktifitas perusahaan yang lebih baik maka pihak manajemen membuka peluang kerja bagi putra-putri bangsa untuk segera bergabung dalam lowongan kerja PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Manufacturing untuk menempati posisi sesuai kebutuhan perusahaan.

<li>Staff Admin</li>

<li>Usia 18 – 22 Tahun</li>

<li>Belum pernah menikah</li>

<li>Berbadan ...</li>
 sehat, bebas Covid-19 dibuktikan dengan Surat Keterangan Hasil Rapid Test Antigen Covid-19 dari Klinik/Rumah Sakit

INFO LOKER BARU | LOWONGAN KERJA PABRIK

PT YAMAHA INDONESIA MOTOR MFG

LOWONGAN KERJA 2023 | Yamaha Group memproduksi kendaraan roda dua dan dipasarkan dengan merek dagang Yamaha.

PT YAMAHA INDONESIA MOTOR MFG berhasil memproduksi serta memasarkan suku cadang dan aksesoris kendaraan.

Hasil produk sepeda motor yang diproduksi oleh PT YIMM adalah Yamaha Mio, Fino, NMAX, Aerox, YZF R15, dan masih banyak lainnya

Guna meningkatkan kinerja dan produktifitas perusahaan yang lebih baik maka pihak manajemen membuka peluang kerja bagi putra-putri bangsa untuk segera bergabung dalam lowongan kerja PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Manufacturing untuk menempati posisi sesuai kebutuhan perusahaan.

Dibutuhkan :
<li>Operator produksi</li>
<li>Operator Gudang</li>
<li>Staff Admin</li>

Kualifikasi Umum :
<li>Usia 18 – 22 Tahun</li>
<li>Pendidikan SMA/SMK/MA atau sederajat</li>
<li>Belum pernah bekerja di PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Manufacturing</li>
<li>Belum pernah menikah</li>
<li>Tidak sedang kuliah</li>
<li>Berbadan ...</li>
 sehat, bebas Covid-19 dibuktikan dengan Surat Keterangan Hasil Rapid Test Antigen Covid-19 dari Klinik/Rumah Sakit
<li>Sudah melakukan vaksin Covid-19 minimal dosis 2 (diutamakan sudah vaksin Booster) dibuktikan dengan Sertifikat Vaksin Covid-19</li>
<li>Tidak pernah terlibat dalam penyalahgunaan narkotika/obat terlarang dan minuman keras</li>

Persyaratan :
<li>Surat lamaran kerja</li>
<li>Daftar riwayat hidup</li>
<li>Fc. ijazah/SKL</li>
<li>Fc. ktp</li>
<li>Fc. Kartu vaksin</li>
<li>Fc kartu keluarga</li>
<li>Fc. SKCK (Yang masih aktif/hidup)</li>
<li>Dan berkas pendukung lainnya.</li>

Fasilitas :
<li>Gaji</li>
<li>seragam</li>
<li>BPJS</li>
<li>Lembur</li>
<li>Jemputan</li>
<li>Dan lain lain</li>

Penempatan Area :
<li>Jakarta</li>
<li>Cikarang</li>
<li>Karawang</li>

LOWONGAN KERJA 2023 | INFO LOWONGAN KERJA

Calon pelamar yang Berminat segera melakukan Pendaftaran secara Online melalui link yang sudah di sediakan oleh perusahaan atau langsung daftar ke Yayasan/ LPTKS atau BKK Yang di percaya/ di tunjuk oleh perusahaan.

Segera Klik Link Dan lengkapi data guna melakukan Pendaftaran :

Applyjobs/career/sma-smk

Bagi pelamar yang sesuai kualifikasi akan segera di panggil melakukan seleksi beserta walk interview.Silakan baca dan cermati dengan semua kriteria yang kami cari sehingga bisa mengikuti seleksi menjadi karyawan di Perusahaan ini.

Sesuaikan kualifikasi diri Anda dengan kriteria tersebut sehingga Anda bisa mengikuti proses seleksi calon pekerja PT YIMM.

Lowongan kerja untuk Operator Produksi dan yang terkait langsung dengan proses produksi dan mesin produksi.

Sehingga tercukupi kebutuhan man power untuk bagian operator produksi dan non produksi (Contoh: bagian logistik dan bagian fasilitas).

Calon karyawan yang lulus seleksi akan segera mendapatkan penempatan kerja sesuai kebutuhan perusahaan.

Bagi karyawan yang kinerja nya bagus ada jenjang karir sehingga bisa menjadi karyawan tetap.

Informasi lowongan kerja selengkapnya segera klik dan cek : INFO LOKER

ALAMAT PERUSAHAAN :
<li>PT YIMM ( PT Yamaha Indonesia Motor Manufacturing ) Jl. DR. KRT. Rajiman Widyodiningrat KM. 23, RT.10/RW.4, Rawa Terate, Cakung, Kota Jakarta Timur, Daerah Khusus Ibukota Jakarta 13920</li>
<li>PT YMMWJ ( PT Yamaha Motor Manufacturing West Java ) Kawasan Industri KIIC, Jl. Permata I Lot BB 1, Puseurjaya, Telukjambe Timur, Puseurjaya, Kec. Telukjambe Tim., Kabupaten Karawang, Jawa Barat 41361</li>
<li>PT YPMI ( PT Yamaha Motor Parts Manufacturing Indonesia ) Kawasan Industri KIIC, Jl. Permata Raya Lot F2 Dan F6, Sukaluyu, Teluk Jambe Timur, Karawang, Jawa Barat 41361</li>

PT YAMAHA INDONESIA MOTOR MANUFACTURING (Bagian Divisi Operasional)
<li>Kawasan Industri MM 2100, Jl. Irian Blok HH No. 1, Jatiwangi, Kec. Cikarang Bar., Bekasi, Jawa Barat 17530</li>

Lowongan kerja bisa di tutup sewaktu waktu jika kebutuhan Karyawan baru di anggap sudah cukup.

<title>Lowongan Kerja 2022 Karyawan Pabrik Lulusan Smk/Sma 2022 | Wilayah... Pt Mayora Indah   Kota Garut, Kota Kulon, Kabupaten Garut, Jawa Barat   </title>
